This includes multi-currency payments, expense reimbursements, and compliant payroll processing in specific MENA countries like the UAE (handling WPS, DEWS, GPSSA, end-of-service benefits), Saudi Arabia (handling WPS, MUDAD, GOSI, end-of-service benefits), and Egypt (handling social security, income tax, martyrs' tax). They offer flexible pro-rata models, consolidated payroll reporting, digital payslips, automated bank verification, and recurring adjustment management. They process multi-currency payroll in over 150 countries.\\n- **Platform:** This is the core infrastructure that connects workforce management with other business functions. Key features include secure access with SSO integration and enterprise-grade access controls, real-time workforce reports with filtering options, role-based access with granular permissions customizable by jurisdiction and location, and complete visibility through activity logs and change history tracking. The platform is mobile-responsive and integrates with various third-party tools like Applicant Tracking Systems (Workday, Greenhouse), Workspace tools (Microsoft, Google), Performance management (Culture Amp), ERP systems (Odoo, Oracle), Communication tools (WhatsApp, Slack), and Finance tools (Quickbooks, Zoho, Xero).\\n- **Compensation Management:** This product focuses on managing multi-currency compensation and contracts. It allows for customizable pay line items (salary, bonuses, allowances, benefits), multi-currency contracts, easy currency conversions, clear history of changes, promotion and appraisal tracking, recurring compensation adjustments, compensation breakdown by country, custom calculations per jurisdiction, and comprehensive benefits breakdown based on local regulations (end-of-service, DEWs, housing).\\n- **Leave Management:** This product provides curated and localized leave policies. It allows for custom leave policies based on location, role, or contract type, with flexibility for half days and working hours. It automatically syncs local and public holidays for over 200 regions and countries. It offers country-specific default policies based on local labor laws and a \\\"Who's Away\\\" calendar for real-time visibility of team absences. It integrates with payroll and offers on-the-go approvals via Cercli Bot (Slack, email).\\n- **Onboarding:** This product streamlines the hiring and onboarding process for employees, contractors, and EORs. It offers automated workflows, centralized document management with secure digital signing, and instant offboarding payouts including end-of-service benefits and unused time off. It provides real-time notifications for key tasks, document expiries, and team introductions via Slack, email, or other preferred channels.\\n- **Documents:** This product focuses on centralized document management with compliance reminders. It allows for secure storage, download, and management of team documents, serving as a single source of truth. It provides timely alerts for renewals, expirations, and missing documents, with automated country-specific templates. It utilizes AI-powered document processing to extract and auto-fill data and offers configurable document requirements by jurisdiction. Notifications are sent via Cercli Bot and email.\\n- **Employer of Record (EOR):** Cercli acts as an EOR, allowing businesses to legally hire, manage, and pay employees in countries where they don't have a legal entity. This helps businesses skip legal complexities, save on overhead costs associated with setting up entities, and handles HR operations like onboarding, compliance, taxes, and benefits.\\n- **Remote Contractors:** Cercli facilitates compliant hiring and payment of remote contractors in multiple currencies. It ensures transparent payments with no hidden fees, auto-generates globally compliant contracts and tax-compliant invoices, and is designed for international expansion by managing the entire workforce in one place.\\n- **Expense Reimbursements:** This product manages expense tracking and approvals, integrating into payroll. It allows managing expenses in any currency with real-time exchange rates, utilizes AI-enabled receipts to extract details, and offers customizable expense categories. It provides automatic or manual payroll sync, fair percentage splits for reimbursements, and approval based on the organization structure. Expenses can be submitted and approved on-the-go via mobile.\\n\\nCercli's market positioning is as a specialized HR and payroll platform for businesses operating in or expanding into the MENA region, while also supporting global teams.
